msg:This time we bought a two-night promotional voucher for a hotel suite, and my friends took time to visit Hangzhou. I want to talk about my experience of this stay here.
The main reason for buying this voucher is its location. It is just a short walk from Hangzhou East Station. You can see the trains entering and leaving the station from the window of the room. Train fans should like it very much, but it is not noisy and very quiet. The room is very large, with one bedroom, one living room and two bathrooms. It is fully equipped and very clean. The window overlooks the boulevard below, and the eyes are full of spring green.
The service here must be praised. Whether it is the front desk, the guest room or the restaurant, they are all very enthusiastic. Before we arrived at the hotel, the front desk n had already contacted us by phone to ask if we had any special requirements. We mentioned that we wanted to add a quilt to each room, and it was solved for us immediately. The front desk lady nodded, and the quick service sister Xiao Yu also went to the room to cover the quilt for us. Because it was almost time for lunch when we arrived, we went to the restaurant on the third floor to order food for lunch. The waiters were about to go off work, but they still received us. Waiter Xiao Gao served us dishes and divided the dishes, and the waiter boy waited until we finished eating before going off work.
Overall, I am very satisfied with staying in this hotel. The only inconvenience is that it is a little far from the West Lake Scenic Area. Fortunately, there are buses and subways at the door, which is convenient, and there are also many taxis.
Hangzhou is a place that can bring you surprises all year round.
